<DESCRIPTION>EXECUTIVE OFFICER INCENTIVE PLAN
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Executive Officer Incentive Plan</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 10.17 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>EXECUTIVE OFFICER INCENTIVE PLAN </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 1 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Purpose </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">The Microsoft Corporation Executive Officer Incentive Plan is intended to provide incentive compensation to executive officers of the Company. Except as provided
in Section&nbsp;4.6, Awards under the Plan are intended to qualify as performance-based compensation under Sections 162(m) and 409A of the Internal Revenue Code. This Plan replaces the Microsoft Corporation Annual Performance Bonus Plan for
Executive Officers for all executive officers effective as of July&nbsp;1, 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 2 </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Definitions </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">The terms used in this Plan include the
feminine as well as the masculine gender and the plural as well as the singular, as the context in which they are used requires. The following terms, unless the context requires otherwise, are defined as follows: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Award&#148;</B> means the incentive compensation awarded by the Committee under Section&nbsp;4.1. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Business Criteria&#148; </B>means the following: sales or licensing volume, revenues, customer satisfaction, expenses, organizational health/productivity, earnings (which includes
similar measurements such as net profits, operating profits and net income, and which may be calculated before or after taxes, interest, depreciation, amortization or taxes), margins, cash flow, shareholder return, return on equity, return on assets
or return on investments, working capital, product shipments or releases, technology advances and innovations, brand or product recognition or acceptance (including market share) and/or stock price. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Code&#148;</B> means the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Committee&#148;</B> means the Compensation Committee of Microsoft Corporation&#146;s Board of Directors. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Company&#148;</B> means Microsoft Corporation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Deferred Compensation Plan&#148;</B> means the Microsoft Corporation Deferred Compensation Plan, or a similar or successor plan or other arrangement for the deferral of compensation
specified by the Committee. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.7</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Participant&#148;</B> means an employee described in Article 3 of the Plan. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.8</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Performance Goals&#148; </B>means the written objective performance goals for Awards under the Plan. To the extent required by Section&nbsp;162(m), the Performance Goals shall be
stated in terms of one or more Business Criteria. Performance Goals may be measured: individually, alternatively or in any combination, including through an index; with respect to the Company, a Company subsidiary, division, business unit, product
line, product or any combination of the foregoing; on an absolute basis, or relative to a target, to a designated comparison group, to results in other periods or to other external measures. The Committee may specify any reasonable definition of the
measures it uses. Such definitions may provide for reasonable adjustments to the measures and may include or exclude items, including but not limited to: extraordinary or unusual and nonrecurring gains or losses, litigation or claim judgments or
settlements, material changes in tax laws, acquisitions or divestitures, the cumulative effect of accounting changes, asset write-downs, restructuring charges, or the results of discontinued operations or products. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.9</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Performance Period&#148;</B> means the period for which an Award is made. Unless otherwise specified by the Committee, the Performance Period shall be a Company fiscal year.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.10</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Plan&#148;</B> means the Microsoft Corporation Executive Officer Incentive Plan, as it may be amended from time to time. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2.11</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>&#147;Section 162(m)&#148;</B> means Code Section&nbsp;162(m) and applicable IRS guidance issued thereunder. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 3 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2"><B>Eligibility and Participation </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">Executive officers of the Company are eligible to receive Awards under the Plan. An executive officer
designated by the Committee to receive an Award under Section&nbsp;4.1 shall be a Participant in the Plan and shall continue to be a Participant until any amounts due under any Awards he may receive have been paid. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 4 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Incentive Awards </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Grants of Awards.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Establishment of Written Terms</B> &#150; Not later than 90 days after the beginning of a Performance Period for which the Committee has determined to grant Awards under the Plan or any
other date required or permitted under Section&nbsp;162(m), the Committee shall determine in writing (a)&nbsp;the Participants receiving Awards for the Performance Period, (b)&nbsp;the Performance Goals for each Participant for the Performance
Period, and (c)&nbsp;the amount payable to a Participant upon attainment of the applicable Performance Goals for the Performance Period. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Incentive Pools</B> &#150; Unless otherwise determined by the Committee, the amount payable to a Participant upon attainment of the applicable Performance Goals for a Performance Period
will be stated as a percentage of an incentive pool. As described in Section&nbsp;4.3 below, the amount of a Participant&#146;s Award may be reduced below the amount determined by multiplying the incentive pool percentage by the incentive pool for
the Performance Period. The total of the incentive pool percentages assigned to all Participants for a Performance Period shall not exceed 100%, and the amount of the incentive pool shall be determined under an objective formula or basis.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Maximum Amount</B> &#150; The maximum amount that may be paid to any Participant based on one or more Performance Periods ending in a fiscal year shall be $20 million.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(d)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>New Executive Officers</B> &#150; The Committee may grant an Award to an individual who becomes an executive officer during a Company fiscal year based on performance during the balance of
the fiscal year or such other Performance Period as it determines. If the Performance Period for such an Award is less than 12 months, within the first 25% of the Performance Period or any other date required or permitted under Section&nbsp;162(m),
the Committee shall determine in writing (a)&nbsp;Performance Goals for the Performance Period, and (b)&nbsp;the amount payable to the Participant upon attainment of the applicable Performance Goals for the Performance Period. The amount payable to
such a Participant upon attainment of the applicable Performance Goals for a Performance Period may be stated as a percentage of an incentive pool. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(e)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>2009 Fiscal Year Awards</B> &#150; The Company&#146;s 2009 fiscal year is a Performance Period for which there will be an incentive pool equal to 0.35% of the Company&#146;s operating
income for the 2009 fiscal year, as reported in the Company&#146;s financial statements (&#147;Operating Income&#148;).<B> </B>The Committee will designate Participants to receive Awards and their incentive pool percentages for this Performance
Period. No payments will be made under an Award described in this paragraph unless the Company&#146;s fiscal year 2009 Operating Income is greater than zero; this positive Operating Income requirement is the Performance Goal for this Performance
Period. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Performance Goal Satisfaction and Certification. </B>Within a reasonable time after the close of a Performance Period, the Committee shall determine whether the Performance Goals
established for that Performance Period have been met. If the Performance Goals have been met, the Committee shall so certify in writing to the extent required by Section&nbsp;162(m). </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Award Amount. </B>If the Committee has made the written certification under Section&nbsp;4.2 for a Performance Period, each Participant to whom the certification applies
shall be eligible to receive a payment under their Award for that Performance Period. For any Performance Period, however, the Committee (and, with respect to Awards for the chief executive officer, two or more independent members of the
Company&#146;s Board </FONT>
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:0%">
<FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">of Directors who are outside directors within the meaning of Section&nbsp;162(m)) shall have the absolute discretion to reduce the amount of, or eliminate entirely,
the payment under an Award to one or more of the Participants. Payment of all or part of an Award amount in the form of an equity compensation grant shall be made under, and subject to the terms and conditions of, the Company&#146;s 2001 Stock Plan
and the applicable grant documentation. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Payment of the Award.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; padding-bottom:3px; margin-top:-2px" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"> <P STYLE="line-height:95%; vertical-align:top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="line-height:95%; vertical-align:top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">Payment of an Award for a Performance Period ending with a Company&#146;s fiscal year shall be made by the end of the fiscal
quarter following the end of the fiscal year. Unless otherwise specified by the Committee, payment of an Award shall be made no later than March&nbsp;15 of the calendar year following the close of the Performance Period (or if later, by the
15</FONT><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="1"><SUP>th</SUP></FONT><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"> day of the third month following the end of the Company&#146;s fiscal year containing the last day of the Performance Period). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">As permitted by the Committee, a Participant may, in accordance with section 409A of the Code, voluntarily defer receipt of an Award in the form of cash under the terms of the Deferred
Compensation Plan. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">The Company shall have the right to deduct from any Award payable in cash any applicable Federal, state and local income and employment taxes and any other amounts that the Company is
required to deduct. Deductions from an Award in the form of an equity compensation award shall be governed by the Company&#146;s 2001 Stock Plan and the applicable grant documentation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Eligibility for Payments.</B> Unless otherwise determined by the Committee, a Participant shall be eligible to receive payment under an Award for a Performance Period only if the
Participant is employed by the Company or a Company subsidiary on the last day of the Performance Period, and only if the Participant satisfies any other conditions to receipt of the Award specified by the Committee. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>4.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Discretionary Awards.</B> The Committee may grant Awards under the Plan that are not intended to qualify as performance-based compensation under Section&nbsp;162(m) and as such will not
need to meet the requirements of this Article 4. Any such Award shall be designated as an Award that is not intended to so qualify in the Award grant documentation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 5 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Administration </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>5.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>General Administration. </B>The Plan is to be administered by the Committee. Subject to the terms and conditions of the Plan, the Committee is authorized and empowered in its sole
discretion to select Participants and to make Awards in such amounts and upon such terms and conditions as it shall determine. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>5.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Administrative Rules. </B>The Committee shall have full power and authority to adopt, amend and rescind administrative guidelines, rules and regulations pertaining to this Plan and to
interpret the Plan and rule on any questions respecting any of its provisions, terms and conditions. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>5.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Decisions Binding. </B>All decisions of the Committee concerning this Plan shall be binding on the Company and its subsidiaries and their respective boards of directors, and on all
Participants and other persons claiming rights under the Plan. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>5.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;162(m) and Shareholder Approval.</B> Other than Awards issued under Section&nbsp;4.6, Awards under this Plan are intended to satisfy the applicable requirements for the
performance-based compensation exception under Section&nbsp;162(m). It is intended that the Plan be administered, interpreted and construed so that such Awards (&#147;162(m) Awards&#148;) meet such requirements. Payments under 162(m) Awards shall be
contingent upon shareholder approval of the material terms of the Plan in accordance with Section&nbsp;162(m). Unless and until such shareholder approval is obtained, no amounts shall be paid under 162(m) Awards. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>5.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Recovery Policy.</B> Amounts paid under the Plan shall be subject to recovery by the Company under its executive compensation recovery policy. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 6 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2"><B>Amendments and Termination </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">The Plan may be amended or terminated by the Committee at any time. All amendments to this Plan,
including an amendment to terminate the Plan, shall be in writing. An amendment shall not be effective without the approval of the shareholders of the Company if such approval is necessary to continue to qualify Awards (other than those issued under
Section&nbsp;4.6) as performance-based compensation under Section&nbsp;162(m), or otherwise under Internal Revenue Service or SEC regulations, the rules of NASDAQ or any other applicable law or regulations. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE 7 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Miscellaneous </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Duration of the Plan. </B>The Plan shall remain in effect until all Performance Periods related to Awards made under the Plan have expired and any payments under such Awards have been
made. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Awards Not Assignable. </B>No Award, or any right thereto, shall be assignable or transferable by a Participant except by will or by the laws of descent and distribution. Any attempted
assignment or alienation shall be void and of no force or effect. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Participant Rights. </B>The right of any Participant to receive any Award payments under the provisions of the Plan shall be an unsecured claim against the general assets of the Company.
The Plan shall not create, nor be construed in any manner as having created, any right by a Participant to any Award for a Performance Period because of a Participant&#146;s participation in the Plan for any prior Performance Period.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Employment at Will.</B> Neither this Plan nor any action or communication under this Plan: (1)&nbsp;gives any employee any right with respect to employment or continuation of current
employment with the Company or its subsidiaries or to employment that is not terminable at will, or (2)&nbsp;sets any employee&#146;s employment with the Company or its subsidiaries for any minimum or fixed period. Employment by the Company or a
Company subsidiary may be terminated by either the employee or the employer at any time, for any reason or no reason, with or without cause, and with or without notice or any kind of pre- or post-termination warning, discipline or procedure. This
Section&nbsp;7.4 applies to employment in the United States. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Successors.</B> Any successor (whether direct or indirect, by purchase, merger, consolidation or otherwise) to all or substantially all of the Company&#146;s business or assets, shall
assume the Company&#146;s liabilities under this Plan and perform any duties and responsibilities in the same manner and to the same extent that the Company would be required to perform if no such succession had taken place.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>References.</B> All statutory and regulatory references in this Plan include successor provisions. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.7</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Severability.</B> If any provision of the Plan is held invalid or illegal for any reason, any illegality or invalidity shall not affect the remaining parts of the Plan, but the Plan shall
be construed and enforced as if the illegal or invalid provision had never been inserted. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>7.8</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Applicable Law and Venue. </B>The Plan shall be governed by the laws of the State of Washington. If the Company or any Participant (or beneficiary) initiates litigation related to this
Plan, the venue for such action will be in King County, Washington. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

defined herein shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Plan.&nbsp;SAs represent the Company&#146;s unfunded and unsecured promise to issue Common Shares at a future date, subject to the terms of this Award Agreement and the
Plan.&nbsp;Awardee has no rights under the SAs other than the rights of a general unsecured creditor of the Company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">2.&nbsp;<I>Vesting of SAs</I>.

the vesting dates set out below, the SAs shall vest as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

or after the applicable vesting date above. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(b)&nbsp;AWARDEE&#146;S RIGHTS IN THE SAs SHALL BE AFFECTED, WITH REGARD TO BOTH VESTING
SCHEDULE AND TERMINATION, BY LEAVES OF ABSENCE, CHANGES IN THE NUMBER OF HOURS WORKED, PARTIAL DISABILITY, AND OTHER CHANGES IN AWARDEE&#146;S EMPLOYMENT STATUS AS PROVIDED IN THE COMPANY&#146;S CURRENT POLICIES IN SUCH MATTERS.&nbsp;ACCOMPANYING
THIS AWARD AGREEMENT IS A CURRENT COPY OF THE COMPANY&#146;S POLICIES IN SUCH MATTERS.&nbsp;THESE POLICIES MAY CHANGE FROM TIME TO TIME WITHOUT NOTICE IN THE COMPANY&#146;S SOLE DISCRETION, AND AWARDEE&#146;S RIGHTS WILL BE GOVERNED BY THE POLICIES
IN EFFECT AT THE TIME OF ANY EMPLOYMENT STATUS CHANGE.&nbsp;E-MAIL &#147;BENEFITS&#148; FOR A COPY OF THE MOST CURRENT POLICIES AT ANY POINT IN TIME. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2">3.&nbsp;<I>Termination</I>.&nbsp;Unless terminated earlier under Section&nbsp;4, 5 or 6 below, an Awardee&#146;s rights under this Award Agreement with respect to the SAs issued under this Award Agreement shall terminate at the time such
SAs are converted into Common Shares and distributed to Awardee. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">4.&nbsp;<I>Termination of Awardee&#146;s Status as a Participant</I>.&nbsp;Except
as otherwise specified in Section&nbsp;5, 6 and 7&nbsp;below, in the event of termination of Awardee&#146;s Continuous Status as a Participant (as such term is defined in Section&nbsp;2(j) of the Plan), Awardee&#146;s rights under this Award
Agreement in any unvested SAs shall terminate.&nbsp;For the avoidance of doubt, an Awardee&#146;s Continuous Status as a Participant terminates at the time Awardee&#146;s actual employer ceases to be the Company or a &#147;Subsidiary&#148; of the
Company, as that term is defined in Section&nbsp;2(y) of the Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">5.&nbsp;<I>Disability of Awardee</I>.&nbsp;Notwithstanding the provisions of
Section&nbsp;4 above, in the event of termination of Awardee&#146;s Continuous Status as a Participant as a result of total and permanent disability (as such term is defined </FONT>
</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">
<FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">in Section&nbsp;12(c) of the Plan), the next vesting date for the SAs, set out in Section&nbsp;2(a), above, shall accelerate by twelve (12)&nbsp;months as of such date
of termination.&nbsp;If Awardee&#146;s disability originally required him or her to take a short-term disability leave that was later converted into long-term disability, then for the purposes of the preceding sentence the date on which Awardee
ceased performing services shall be deemed to be the date of commencement of the short-term disability leave.&nbsp;Awardee&#146;s rights in any unvested SAs that remain unvested after the application of this Section&nbsp;5 shall terminate at the
time Awardee ceases to be in Continuous Status as a Participant. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">6.&nbsp;<I>Death of Awardee</I>.&nbsp;Notwithstanding the provisions of
Section&nbsp;4 above, in the event of the death of Awardee: (a)&nbsp;If Awardee is, at the time of death, in Continuous Status as a Participant, the next vesting date for the SAs, set out in Section&nbsp;2(a) above, shall accelerate by twelve
(12)&nbsp;months as of the date of death. (b)&nbsp;Awardee&#146;s rights in any unvested SAs that remain after the application of Section&nbsp;6(a) shall terminate at the time of Awardee&#146;s death. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">7.&nbsp;<I>Retirement of Awardee</I>.&nbsp;Notwithstanding the provisions of Section&nbsp;4 above, in the event of Awardee&#146;s Retirement, Awardee shall be
treated as continuously employed through the vesting periods in Section&nbsp;2(a) above.&nbsp;For this purpose, &#147;Retirement&#148; means termination of employment with the Company or its direct and indirect subsidiaries after the earlier of
(a)&nbsp;age 65, or (b)&nbsp;attaining age 55 and 15 years of Continuous Service, provided that immediately prior to termination of employment the Awardee is employed by Microsoft (or its direct and indirect subsidiaries) in the United
States.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">This Section&nbsp;7 will only apply to a Retirement if (a)&nbsp;the Retirement is more than one year after August&nbsp;29,
20&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, (b)&nbsp;Awardee executes a release in conjunction with the Retirement in the form provided by the Company, and (c)&nbsp;Awardee&#146;s employment does not terminate due to misconduct (as determined in the sole discretion
of the Company&#146;s senior corporate officer in charge of the Human Resources department), including but not limited to misconduct in violation of Company policy and misconduct that adversely affects the Company&#146;s interests or reputation.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">For purposes of this Section&nbsp;7, &#147;Continuous Service&#148; means that Awardee has continuously remained an employee of the Company or its
direct and indirect subsidiaries, measured from Awardee&#146;s &#147;most recent hire date&#148; as reflected in the Company records.&nbsp;For an Awardee who became an employee of the Company following the acquisition of his or her employer by the
Company or its direct or indirect subsidiaries, service with the acquired employer shall count toward Continuous Service, and Continuous Service shall be measured from Awardee&#146;s acquired company hire date as reflected in the Company&#146;s
records. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">8. <I>Value of Unvested SAs</I>.&nbsp;In consideration of the award of these SAs, Awardee agrees that upon and following termination of
Awardee&#146;s Continuous Status as a Participant for any reason (whether or not in breach of applicable laws), and regardless of whether Awardee is terminated with or without cause, notice, or pre-termination procedure or whether Awardee asserts or
prevails on a claim that Awardee&#146;s employment was terminable only for cause or only with notice or pre-termination procedure, any unvested SAs under this Award Agreement shall be deemed to have a value of zero dollars ($0.00). </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">9.&nbsp;<I>Conversion of SAs to Common Shares; Responsibility for Taxes</I>. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(a)&nbsp;Provided Awardee has satisfied the requirements of Section&nbsp;9(b) below, on the vesting of any SAs, such vested SAs shall be converted
into an equivalent number of Common Shares that will be distributed to Awardee within 90 days after the date of the vesting event, or in the event of Awardee&#146;s death, to Awardee&#146;s legal representative within 90 days after date of death;
provided that SAs that vest on &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, 20&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, shall be converted into an equivalent number of Common Shares that
will be distributed to Awardee (1)&nbsp;after the number of SAs subject to this Award Agreement is determined, and (2)&nbsp;between August&nbsp;31 and September&nbsp;30, 20&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;. Notwithstanding the foregoing, if accelerated
vesting of an SA occurs pursuant to a provision of the Plan not addressed in this Award Agreement, distribution of the related Common Share shall not occur until the date distribution would have occurred under this Award Agreement absent such
accelerated vesting. The distribution to Awardee, or in the case of Awardee&#146;s death, to Awardee&#146;s legal representative, of Common Shares in respect of the vested SAs shall be evidenced by a stock certificate, </FONT>
</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%">
<FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">appropriate entry on the books of the Company or of a duly authorized transfer agent of the Company, or other appropriate means as determined by the Company.&nbsp;In
the event ownership or issuance of Common Shares is not feasible due to applicable exchange controls, securities regulations, tax laws or other provisions of applicable law, as determined by the Company in its sole discretion, Awardee, or in the
event of Awardee&#146;s death, Awardee&#146;s legal representative, shall receive cash proceeds in an amount equal to the value of the Common Shares otherwise distributable to Awardee, as determined by the Company in its sole discretion, net of
amounts withheld in satisfaction of the requirements of Section&nbsp;9(b) below. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(b)&nbsp;Regardless of any action the Company or
Awardee&#146;s actual employer takes with respect to any or all income tax (including federal, state and local taxes), social insurance, payroll tax, payment on account, or other tax-related withholding items (&#147;Tax-Related Items&#148;) that
arise in connection with the SAs, Awardee acknowledges and agrees that the ultimate liability for any Tax-Related Items determined by the Company in its discretion to be legally due by Awardee, is and remains Awardee&#146;s responsibility. Awardee
acknowledges and agrees that the Company and/or Awardee&#146;s actual employer (i)&nbsp;make no representations or undertakings regarding the treatment of any Tax-Related Items in connection with any aspect of the SAs, including the grant of the
SAs, the vesting of SAs, the conversion of the SAs into Common Shares or the receipt of an equivalent cash payment, the subsequent sale of any Common Shares acquired and the receipt of any dividends; and (ii)&nbsp;do not commit to and are under no
obligation to structure the terms of the grant or any aspect of the SAs to reduce or eliminate Awardee&#146;s liability for any Tax-Related Items. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">Prior to the relevant taxable or tax-withholding event, as applicable, Awardee shall pay, or make adequate arrangements satisfactory to the Company or to Awardee&#146;s actual employer (in their sole discretion) to satisfy all
obligations for Tax-Related Items.&nbsp;In this regard, Awardee authorizes the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer to withhold all applicable Tax-Related Items from Awardee&#146;s wages or other cash compensation payable to Awardee by the
Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer.&nbsp;Alternatively, or in addition, the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer may, in their sole discretion, and without notice to or authorization by Awardee, (i)&nbsp;sell or arrange for the sale of
Common Shares to be issued upon the vesting of SAs or other event to satisfy the withholding obligation, and/or (ii)&nbsp;withhold in Common Shares, provided that the Company and Awardee&#146;s actual employer shall withhold only the amount of
shares necessary to satisfy the minimum withholding amount or such other amount determined by the Company as not resulting in negative accounting consequences for the Company. Awardee will be deemed to have been issued the full number of Common
Shares subject to the SAs, notwithstanding that a number of whole vested Common Shares are held back solely for the purpose of paying the Tax-Related Items.&nbsp;Awardee shall pay to the Company or to Awardee&#146;s actual employer any amount of
Tax-Related Items that the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer may be required to withhold as a result of Awardee&#146;s receipt of SAs, the vesting of SAs, or the conversion of vested SAs to Common Shares that cannot be satisfied by the means
described in this paragraph.&nbsp;Except where applicable legal or regulatory provisions prohibit and notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, the standard process for the payment of an Awardee&#146;s Tax-Related Items shall be for the
Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer to withhold in Common Shares only to the amount of shares necessary to satisfy the minimum withholding amount or such other amount determined by the Company as not resulting in negative accounting
consequences for the Company.&nbsp;The Company may refuse to deliver Common Shares to Awardee if Awardee fails to comply with Awardee&#146;s obligation in connection with the Tax-Related Items as described in this section 9. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(c)&nbsp;In lieu of issuing fractional Common Shares, on the vesting of a fraction of a SA, the Company shall round the shares to the nearest whole
share and any such share that represents a fraction of a SA will be included in a subsequent vest date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(d)&nbsp;Until the
distribution to Awardee of the Common Shares in respect of the vested SAs is evidenced by a stock certificate, appropriate entry on the books of the Company or of a duly authorized transfer agent of the Company, or other appropriate means, Awardee
shall have no right to vote or receive dividends or any other rights as a shareholder with respect to such Common Shares, notwithstanding the vesting of SAs.&nbsp;No adjustment will be made for a dividend or other right for which the record date is
prior to the date Awardee is recorded as the owner of the Common Shares, except as provided in Section&nbsp;14 of the Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2">(e)&nbsp;By accepting the Award of SAs evidenced by this Award Agreement, Awardee agrees not to sell any of the Common Shares received on account of vested SAs at a time when applicable laws or Company </FONT>
</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%">
<FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">policies prohibit a sale.&nbsp;This restriction shall apply so long as Awardee is an Employee, Consultant or outside director of the Company or a Subsidiary of the
Company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">10.&nbsp;<I>Non-Transferability of SAs</I>.&nbsp;Awardee&#146;s right in the SAs awarded under this Award Agreement and any interest
therein may not be sold, pledged, assigned, hypothecated, transferred, or disposed of in any manner, other than by will or by the laws of descent or distribution.&nbsp;SAs shall not be subject to execution, attachment or other process. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">11.&nbsp;<I>Acknowledgment of Nature of Plan and SAs</I>.&nbsp;In accepting the Award, Awardee acknowledges that: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(a)&nbsp;the Plan is established voluntarily by the Company, it is discretionary in nature and may be modified, amended, suspended or terminated by
the Company at any time, as provided in the Plan; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(b)&nbsp;the Award of SAs is voluntary and occasional and does not create any
contractual or other right to receive future awards of SAs or other awards, or benefits in lieu of SAs even if SAs have been awarded repeatedly in the past; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(c)&nbsp;all decisions with respect to SAs or other future awards, if any, will be at the sole discretion of the Company; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(d)&nbsp;Awardee&#146;s participation in the Plan is voluntary; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(e)&nbsp;the future value of the underlying Common Shares is unknown and cannot be predicted with certainty; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(f)&nbsp;if Awardee receives Common Shares, the value of such Common Shares acquired on vesting of SAs may increase or decrease in value;
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(g)&nbsp;notwithstanding any terms or conditions of the Plan to the contrary and consistent with Section&nbsp;4, above, in the event
of termination of Awardee&#146;s Continuous Status as a Participant under circumstances where Section&nbsp;7 does not apply (whether or not in breach of applicable laws), Awardee&#146;s right to receive SAs and vest under the Plan, if any, will
terminate effective as of the date that Awardee is no longer actively employed and will not be extended by any notice period mandated under applicable law. Awardee&#146;s right to receive Common Shares pursuant to the SAs after termination of
Continuous Status as a Participant, if any, will be calculated as of the date of termination of Awardee&#146;s active employment and will not be extended by any notice period mandated under applicable law. The senior corporate officer in charge of
the Human Resources department shall have the exclusive discretion to determine when Awardee is no longer actively employed for purposes of the award of SAs; and </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">(h)&nbsp;Awardee acknowledges and agrees that, regardless of whether Awardee is terminated with or without cause, notice or pre-termination
procedure or whether Awardee asserts or prevails on a claim that Awardee&#146;s employment was terminable only for cause or only with notice or pre-termination procedure, Awardee has no right to, and will not bring any legal claim or action for,
(a)&nbsp;any damages for any portion of the SAs that have been vested and converted into Common Shares, or (b)&nbsp;termination of any unvested SAs under this Award Agreement.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">12.&nbsp;<I>No Employment Right</I>.&nbsp;Awardee acknowledges that neither the fact of this Award of SAs nor any provision of this Award Agreement or the Plan or
the policies adopted pursuant to the Plan shall confer upon Awardee any right with respect to employment or continuation of current employment with the Company or with Awardee&#146;s actual employer, or to employment that is not terminable at
will.&nbsp;Awardee further acknowledges and agrees that neither the Plan nor this Award of SAs makes Awardee&#146;s employment with the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer for any minimum or fixed period, and that such employment is subject to
the mutual consent of Awardee and the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer, and may be terminated by either Awardee or the Company or Awardee&#146;s actual employer at any time, for any reason or no reason, with or without cause or notice or
any kind of pre- or post-termination warning, discipline or procedure. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">13.&nbsp;<I>Administration</I>.&nbsp;The authority to manage and control the
operation and administration of this Award Agreement shall be vested in the Committee (as such term is defined in Section&nbsp;2(f) of the Plan), and the Committee shall have all powers and discretion with respect to this Award Agreement as it has
with respect to </FONT>
</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">
<FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">the Plan.&nbsp;Any interpretation of the Award Agreement by the Committee and any decision made by the Committee with respect to the Award Agreement shall be final and
binding on all parties. References to the Committee in this Award Agreement shall be read to include a reference to any delegate of the Committee acting within the scope of his or her delegation. </FONT></P> <P

terms of the Plan, and this Award Agreement is subject to all interpretations, amendments, rules and regulations promulgated by the Committee from time to time pursuant to the Plan. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">15.&nbsp;<I>Notices</I>.&nbsp;Any written notices provided for in this Award Agreement that are sent by mail shall be deemed received three business days after
mailing, but not later than the date of actual receipt.&nbsp;Notices shall be directed, if to Awardee, at Awardee&#146;s address indicated by the Company&#146;s records and, if to the Company, at the Company&#146;s principal executive office.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">16.&nbsp;<I>Electronic Delivery</I>.&nbsp;The Company may, in its sole discretion, decide to deliver any documents related to SAs awarded under the
Plan or future SAs that may be awarded under the Plan by electronic means or request Awardee&#146;s consent to participate in the Plan by electronic means.&nbsp;Awardee hereby consents to receive such documents by electronic delivery and agrees to
participate in the Plan through an on-line or electronic system established and maintained by the Company or another third party designated by the Company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial"

the other documents referenced in the preceding sentence, as the latter may be amended from time to time in the Company&#146;s sole discretion. Awardee further acknowledges that Awardee must accept this Award Agreement in the manner prescribed by
the Company no later than the earlier of the first anniversary of Award Date or the first vesting date specified in Section&nbsp;2(a) of this Award Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT

not already been approved, the Company agrees to submit this Award for approval as soon as practical.&nbsp;If such approval is not obtained, this award is null and void. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT

Awardee.&nbsp;Awardee agrees not to rely on any oral information regarding this Award of SAs or any written materials not identified in this Section&nbsp;21. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 31.1 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Arial"
SIZE="2"><B>CERTIFICATIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">I, Steven A. Ballmer, certify that: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial"

</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">3. Based on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information included in this report, fairly present in all material respects
the financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of the registrant as of, and for, the periods presented in this report; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">4. The

in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for the registrant and have: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">a) Designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or
caused such disclosure controls and procedures to be designed under our supervision, to ensure that material information relating to the registrant, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by others within those entities,
particularly during the period in which this report is being prepared; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">b) Designed such internal control over financial reporting, or
caused such internal control over financial reporting to be designed under our supervision, to provide reasonable assurance regarding the reliability of financial reporting and the preparation of financial statements for external purposes in
accordance with generally accepted accounting principles; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">c) Evaluated the effectiveness of the registrant&#146;s disclosure controls
and procedures and presented in this report our conclusions about the effectiveness of the disclosure controls and procedures, as of the end of the period covered by this report based on such evaluation; and </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">d) Disclosed in this report any change in the registrant&#146;s internal control over financial reporting that occurred during the registrant&#146;s
most recent fiscal quarter (the registrant&#146;s fourth fiscal quarter in the case of an annual report) that has materially affected, or is reasonably likely to materially affect, the registrant&#146;s internal control over financial reporting; and
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">5. The registrant&#146;s other certifying officer and I have disclosed, based on our most recent evaluation of internal control over financial
reporting, to the registrant&#146;s auditors and the audit committee of registrant&#146;s board of directors (or persons performing the equivalent functions): </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Arial" SIZE="2">a) All significant deficiencies and material weaknesses in the design or operation of internal control over financial reporting which are reasonably
